\index{vvenc@{vvenc}!\_byteStreamNALUnit@{\_byteStreamNALUnit}}
\index{\_byteStreamNALUnit@{\_byteStreamNALUnit}!vvenc@{vvenc}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{\_byteStreamNALUnit()}{\_byteStreamNALUnit()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily static void vvenc\+::\+\_\+byte\+Stream\+N\+A\+L\+Unit (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classvvenc_1_1InputByteStream}{Input\+Byte\+Stream}} \&}]{bs,  }\item[{std\+::vector$<$ uint8\+\_\+t $>$ \&}]{nal\+Unit,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structvvenc_1_1AnnexBStats}{Annex\+B\+Stats}} \&}]{stats }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}

Parse an A\+VC AnnexB Bytestream bs to extract a single nal\+Unit while accumulating bytestream statistics into stats.

If E\+OF occurs while trying to extract a N\+A\+Lunit, an exception of std\+::ios\+\_\+base\+::failure is thrown. The contsnts of stats will be correct at this point.

\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespacevvenc_a00c21d60c8584d88cc2e7d6817bd2a8f}\label{namespacevvenc_a00c21d60c8584d88cc2e7d6817bd2a8f}} 
\index{vvenc@{vvenc}!calcMD5@{calcMD5}}
\index{calcMD5@{calcMD5}!vvenc@{vvenc}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{calcMD5()}{calcMD5()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily uint32\+\_\+t calc\+M\+D5 (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacevvenc_aab58447b4769df54b9659420fcbb321b}{C\+Pel\+Unit\+Buf}} \&}]{pic,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structvvenc_1_1PictureHash}{Picture\+Hash}} \&}]{digest,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structvvenc_1_1BitDepths}{Bit\+Depths}} \&}]{bit\+Depths }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Calculate the M\+D5sum of pic, storing the result in digest. \mbox{\hyperlink{classvvenc_1_1MD5}{M\+D5}} calculation is performed on Y\textquotesingle{} then Cb, then Cr; each in raster order. Pel data is inserted into the \mbox{\hyperlink{classvvenc_1_1MD5}{M\+D5}} function in little-\/endian byte order, using sufficient bytes to represent the picture bitdepth. Eg, 10bit data uses little-\/endian two byte words; 8bit data uses single byte words.
